 You will be surprised to know that in the capital of Delhi alone where ten thousand cases of cybercrime are happening in a day, the Central Government has stopped the cyber tribunal set up for cybercrime
 dukhad ye bhi he ki pichley saat saal se chairman ke naa hone se is tribunel main 2011 se ek bhi maamle kii sunwaayee nahin ho saki
 In this era of information technology where cybercrime is steadily growing and everyone of you and us who use smart mobiles is an easy victim, the government has scrapped the Cyber appellate Tribunal in 2006
 is tribunel main 2011 se chairman naa hone se sibar krime se jude ek bhi maamle kii sunwaayee nahin ho saki thi
 That is, if you suddenly lose millions of rupees from a bank account or someone has stolen your personal information from a computer, or someone has hacked your computer, then you will not be able to do anything to get their hearing and to punish the offender
 aapke paas haath malane ke alaava koi or vikalp nahin he
 Cyber expert Pawan Duggal explains that only the case registers in the Crime Bureau's crime records that register firs and the total number of crime cases which are perpetrated are completely opposite to current reality
 hamane kuch saal pehle ek survey kiya tha ki bharat main kis tarah se under reporting hoti he, sibar krime ke maamalon main hamane paaya ki 500 main se 50 kii hi shikaayat milti he or phir 50 main se 1 cese kii hi exiaar darj ho paati he
 At present, the government has merged the Cyber tribunal and the Airport Tribunal into the TD set ie Telecom Disputes Settlement and Appellate Tribunal, but it is only a ritual payment because TD Set already has one and a half thousand cases pending and only to hear the cases
 There is a bench
